2025-06-01T02:11:18.8620326Z         This leads to an ambiguous overall configuration. If you want to distribute this
2025-06-01T02:11:18.8620700Z         package, please make sure that 'mypyc.external.googletest.src' is explicitly added
2025-06-01T02:11:18.8620840Z         to the `packages` configuration field.
2025-06-01T02:11:18.8620853Z 
2025-06-01T02:11:18.8621018Z         Alternatively, you can also rely on setuptools' discovery methods
2025-06-01T02:11:18.8621287Z         (for example by using `find_namespace_packages(...)`/`find_namespace:`
2025-06-01T02:11:18.8621457Z         instead of `find_packages(...)`/`find:`).
2025-06-01T02:11:18.8621466Z 
2025-06-01T02:11:18.8621810Z         You can read more about "package discovery" on setuptools documentation page:
2025-06-01T02:11:18.8621823Z 
2025-06-01T02:11:18.8622134Z         - https://setuptools.pypa.io/en/latest/userguide/package_discovery.html
2025-06-01T02:11:18.8622143Z 
2025-06-01T02:11:18.8622585Z         If you don't want 'mypyc.external.googletest.src' to be distributed and are
2025-06-01T02:11:18.8622882Z         already explicitly excluding 'mypyc.external.googletest.src' via
2025-06-01T02:11:18.8623189Z         `find_namespace_packages(...)/find_namespace` or `find_packages(...)/find`,
2025-06-01T02:11:18.8623502Z         you can try to use `exclude_package_data`, or `include-package-data=False` in
2025-06-01T02:11:18.8623689Z         combination with a more fine grained `package-data` configuration.
2025-06-01T02:11:18.8623694Z 
2025-06-01T02:11:18.8624016Z         You can read more about "package data files" on setuptools documentation page:
2025-06-01T02:11:18.8624026Z 
2025-06-01T02:11:18.8624499Z         - https://setuptools.pypa.io/en/latest/userguide/datafiles.html
2025-06-01T02:11:18.8624514Z 
2025-06-01T02:11:18.8624520Z 
2025-06-01T02:11:18.8624818Z         [^1]: For Python, any directory (with suitable naming) can be imported,
2025-06-01T02:11:18.8625003Z               even if it does not contain any `.py` files.
2025-06-01T02:11:18.8625273Z               On the other hand, currently there is no concept of package data
2025-06-01T02:11:18.8625502Z               directory, all directories are treated like packages.
2025-06-01T02:11:18.8625648Z         ********************************************************************************
2025-06-01T02:11:18.8625824Z 
2025-06-01T02:11:18.8625970Z !!
